[38;5;130m291 [mRank INT
[38;5;130m292 [m);
[38;5;130m293 
294 [m[34m-- add the top three cars for each make into a table[m
[38;5;130m295 INSERT[m [35mINTO[m Top_Three(Car_ID, Make, Total, Rank)
[38;5;130m296 SELECT[m * [35mFROM[m Rank_Table1 [38;5;130mUNION[m [38;5;130mSELECT[m * [35mFROM[m Rank_Table2 [38;5;130mUNION[m [38;5;130mSELECT[m * [35mFROM[m Rank_Table3 [35mORDER[m [35mBY[m Make, Rank1;
[38;5;130m297 
298 [m[34m-- save the top three of each car make to a file[m
[38;5;130m299 SELECT[m * [35mFROM[m Top_Three;
[38;5;130m300 
301 [m[34m-- drop unused tables[m
[38;5;130m302 DROP[m [35mTABLE[m [35mIF[m [38;5;130mEXISTS[m Rank_Table1;
[38;5;130m303 DROP[m [35mTABLE[m [35mIF[m [38;5;130mEXISTS[m Rank_Table2;
[38;5;130m304 DROP[m [35mTABLE[m [35mIF[m [38;5;130mEXISTS[m Rank_Table3;
[38;5;130m305 
306 [m[34m/* 3 */[m
[38;5;130m307 
308 [m[34m-- declare output file[m
[38;5;130m309 [m.headers [35mON[m
[38;5;130m310 [m.[35mmode[m csv
[38;5;130m311 [m.output extract3.csv
[38;5;130m312 
313 [m[34m-- create table to hold updated Judges info[m
[38;5;130m314 DROP[m [35mTABLE[m [35mIF[m [38;5;130mEXISTS[m Updated_Judges;
[38;5;130m315 CREATE[m [35mTABLE[m Updated_Judges(
[38;5;130m316 [mJudge_ID TEXT,
[38;5;130m317 [mJudge_Name TEXT,
[38;5;130m318 [mNum_Cars INT,
[38;5;130m319 [mStart_Timestamp DATETIME,
[38;5;130m320 [mEnd_Timestamp DATETIME,
[38;5;130m321 [mDuration DATETIME,
[38;5;130m322 [mAverage REAL
[38;5;130m323 [m);
[38;5;130m324 
325 [m[34m-- add data to the Updated_Judges table using a single query[m
[38;5;130m326 SELECT[m Judge_ID, Judge_Name,
[38;5;130m327 [mCOUNT(Timestamp) [35mAS[m Num_Cars,
[38;5;130m328 [mMIN(Timestamp) [35mAS[m Start_Timestamp,
[38;5;130m329 [mMAX(Timestamp) [35mAS[m End_Timestamp,
[38;5;130m330 [mCAST((JULIANDAY(MAX(Timestamp)) - JULIANDAY(MIN(Timestamp)))*[31m24[m [35mAS[m INT) [35mAS[m  Duration_Hrs,
[38;5;130m331 [mCAST(((JULIANDAY(MAX(Timestamp)) - JULIANDAY(MIN(Timestamp)))*[31m24[m*[31m60[m) [35mAS[m INT) / COUNT(Timestamp) [35mas[m Average_Min_Per_Car
[38;5;130m332 [m[35mFROM[m Judges [35mGROUP[m [35mBY[m Judge_ID;
[38;5;130m333
